# Performance tuning | SolanaMevBot

Make sure you already have the bot running and landing before diving into this page. This page assumes you already have some basic knowledge of the bot.

Once you get your bot up and running, the next step is to tune it to get the best performance. There are a lot of variables so the exact config may differ for every person. This page will go through all the things that may affect the performance, and how you can improve it.

When an arb opportunity appears, there will be hundreds or thousands of bots trying to seize it. And you want to be faster than others and be the first few ones to take it. So the overall idea is very simple, you want to be fast in every possible places. Fast reading, fast sending, fast landing etc. And all the tuning in this page is around this. every milliseconds matters.

Make sure you only tweak one or just a few configs at a time, verify your change works, then repeat. If you change too many things at once it's very hard to figure out what goes wrong.

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/performance-tuning#rpc)

RPC


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

RPC is probably one of the most important things for your setup. There are a few things to consider here.

### 

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/performance-tuning#location)

location

location can affect the performance in several different ways. First you want your server to be as close to your RPC as possible. The easiest way to test is ping your rpc address from your server.

Example:

Copy

    ping api.mainnet-beta.solana.com

The ideal value for a good location is <10 ms. The most idea location is <1 ms, which basically means your RPC is physically located in the same data center as your server.

### 

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/performance-tuning#read-vs-send)

Read vs Send

Read and send are actually two totally different things for an RPC. Find a good read RPC to read can make sure you get the opportunity right when it appears, a good send RPC can help you to land the transaction and land it fast.

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/performance-tuning#read-tuning)

Read tuning


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

_**PROCESS\_DELAY**_

Default is 1000, unit in milliseconds. This controls how long the bot wait to quote and try to find an arb again for a given base mint + trade size. The less of this, the more frequently the bot try to find the arb. Do note that a small number like 100 may kill your RPC or Jup API due to the high load of requests. If you make this smaller and then sees much less or no opportunities, that means it's too small and you need to adjust it.

If you are using public jup api [https://quote-api.jup.ag/v6](https://quote-api.jup.ag/v6)
, make sure you set PROCESS\_DELAY to a very big number like 10000, with only one base mint and one trade size, this may help you to test it longer before getting blocked.

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/performance-tuning#send-tuning)

Send tuning


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/performance-tuning#enable_spam)

**ENABLE\_SPAM**

For maximum profit you will want to enable this. This means the bot will send transactions to all the senders you set, some of them may not land, some may land but failed, and some will land and succeed. You will need to find a good RPC and tweak your settings to make sure your profit can cover all the gas fees for failed transactions.

### 

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/performance-tuning#skip_preflight)

**SKIP\_PREFLIGHT**

This is a config you can change when you send your transaction. To understand what it means you can read the Solana doc [here](https://solana.com/docs/advanced/retry#the-cost-of-skipping-preflight)
. In short the rpc you send your transaction with will simulate your transaction and not sending it if it failed. This is very similar to ENABLE\_SIMULATION, but this runs with your send rpcs, and ENABLE\_SIMULATION runs with your read rpc.

You should only set at most one of ENABLE\_SIMULATION=true and SKIP\_PREFLIGHT=false. Setting both is a waste of rpc resources.

### 

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/performance-tuning#send_rpc_urls)

**SEND\_RPC\_URLS**

It is recommended to find multiple RPCs for sending, as they can land in different situations, and you want whoever is the fastest to land it for you. You can use the following tool to test how fast a RPC is to land a transaction to help you find the best ones:

[https://github.com/Cetipoo/solana-rpc-benchmark-tool](https://github.com/Cetipoo/solana-rpc-benchmark-tool)

### 

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/performance-tuning#use_different_tx_for_senders)

**USE\_DIFFERENT\_TX\_FOR\_SENDERS**

By default, the bot will send the same transaction through all the senders. This can make sure the fastest land it and if it failed, you only lose one gas fee. When set `USE_DIFFERENT_TX_FOR_SENDERS=true`, the bot will use a different transaction for different senders. This will give you more profit if the oppotunity is big enough to allow more than one, but also will lose you more gas fee if all are failed.

### 

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/performance-tuning#compute_unit_price)

**COMPUTE\_UNIT\_PRICE**

aka priority fee on solana. Default to 10001, which based on helius lab, is the minimum number that some validators will not drop your transaction.

In theory, the higher this is, the more likely your transaction can land and the faster it will land. But, this will result in higher gas fee as well. So you need to adjust this carefully and maybe in small incremental values to find the best value for your setup.

You can also use the tool to test different COMPUTE\_UNIT\_PRICE value to help you decide which one is better, do note that running the test will cost you gas fee for all the ones that landed:

[https://github.com/Cetipoo/solana-rpc-benchmark-tool](https://github.com/Cetipoo/solana-rpc-benchmark-tool)

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/performance-tuning#jito)

Jito


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Jito is a mev service on Solana, that allows you to send transaction with a tip, which will help you land faster, and it will ONLY land it if it succeeded. Which means no failed transaction will be landed! Hence no lose on gas fee! To learn more about jito, you can read here: [https://www.jito.wtf/](https://www.jito.wtf/)

### 

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/performance-tuning#enable_jito)

**ENABLE\_JITO**

When you set ENABLE\_JITO=true, the bot will send the transaction through jito. This is basically a no brainer and should always be set. Jito does have a 50/s/ip rate limit, so if you are seeing too many opportunities that above this number, some may not go through with jito due to rate limit.

When using Jito, the transaction is not send through RPC, but send through Jito block engine. The bot will send the transaction to all 5 jito block engine, you want to be very close to at least one of them to minimize your sending time. [https://jito-labs.gitbook.io/mev/searcher-resources/block-engine/mainnet-addresses](https://jito-labs.gitbook.io/mev/searcher-resources/block-engine/mainnet-addresses)

### 

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/performance-tuning#jito_tip_bp)

**JITO\_TIP\_BP**

Default to 5000, this means 50% of your profit will be used as the tip to Jito, which helps you to land the transaction. Jito runs an auction house on each Jito leader, and will order all the jito bundle by the tip they give. So in theory, if you and another person both try to seize the same opportunity, and you have a higher tip than the other person, you will be ranked higher and take the oppotunity and the other person will fail to get it. Though in reality there's a lot more to how Jito works, and higher tip does not always mean higher landing rate. This is something you should tweak and find the best number for your own setup.

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/performance-tuning#jupiter-api)

Jupiter API


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The bot provides a convenient way to run the Jupiter(V6) API direclty with the bot when setting the JUPITER\_URL to `http://0.0.0.0:18080`. But you can also choose to host it yourself, or find a third party provider. As all the tuning we are doing here, our goal is to be fast. This tuning guide is mostly for the Jupiter API hosted together with the bot.

### 

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/performance-tuning#yellowstone_url)

**YELLOWSTONE\_URL**

Yellowstone(grpc) is a geyser plugin for Solana validator. You may see people talking about yellowstone/grpc/geyser, they are all the same thing. Read more here: [https://docs.triton.one/project-yellowstone/introduction](https://docs.triton.one/project-yellowstone/introduction)
 It provides a stream service that will push the data continually to the receiver. To run a high performance Jupiter API, this is something you must have. With this you may be able to run a Jupiter API with up to 1000 different mints. Without it, you will have a hard time to run even with 50 different mints.

To debug and see how your yellowstone performs, run `debug.sh` instead of `run.sh`, which will output some additional logs for jupiter. Pay attention to the logs like the following:

For the most performant yellowstone, you should barely see this log. You can see there's a lagging min and max number. If the difference is less than 10-20, it's usually still ok, if it's more then you may likely not getting any opportunity with it.

### 

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/performance-tuning#rpc_url)

**RPC\_URL**

Jupiter needs a normal rpc to read a few things. In addition, if you do not provide a YELLOWSTONE\_URL, the bot will run Jupiter API in pull mode, which means it will make a huge amount of requests every few seconds. This can be a huge amount for some RPC, and you will see Jupiter crash or too many requests error if you have too many intermedium mints.

You should never use more than 50 mints for your intermedium mints when you don't have `YELLOWSTONE_URL`. And 50 is for a very good rpc. Most rpc can only affort it to be 3-10

### 

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/performance-tuning#use_direct_route_only)

USE\_DIRECT\_ROUTE\_ONLY

When set to true, the bot will only look for 2hop(A -> B -> A) trade. Setting to true will lead to shorter quote time to Jupiter API, which end up with faster landing. When setting to false, the bot will also look for opportunities like (A -> B -> C -> A). Setting to false will lead to more opportunities, but taking more time to quote.

### 

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/performance-tuning#jup_max_accounts)

**JUP\_MAX\_ACCOUNTS**

This is used when quoting from Jupiter API. A solana transaction can contain at most 64 accounts. With the help of AddressLookupTable this number can go up.

The bot will quote twice for each mint, A ->B and B -> A. So the total accounts used will be 2 \* JUP\_MAX\_ACCOUNTS in worst case.

For the bot specifically, you shouldn't try to go higher than 32 for the value. The higher the value is, the more complicated route it can found, but slower. With lower value, you will find less route but faster.

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/performance-tuning#intermedium-mints)

Intermedium mints


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3811539071-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fx2rxpD03KDvMgJqIkdla%252Fuploads%252FXgYe4dm2NOvEFWmqble5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dca591b4b-5130-4d29-b60c-e877325ea0ef&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=89bcfc56&sv=2)

A good token choice makes a huge difference

One of the biggest diffrenciation between different strategies is how you choose your intermedium mints.

In general, the more intermedium mints you have, the slower your Jupiter quote will be. But also the more intermedium mints you have, the more chances you may find opportunities. So you will need to test for different combinations and find what works best for you.

### 

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/performance-tuning#intermedium_mint_count_from_birdeye)

**INTERMEDIUM\_MINT\_COUNT\_FROM\_BIRDEYE**

This param configs how many top MINTS to use as intermedium mints. The mints are also pulled fro Birdeye. If you have too many intermedium tokens, it can slow down your jupiter quote because it's overloaded. So try a few different values and see which one works best for you.

Note: This should be equal or smaller than _**JUPITER\_TOKEN\_COUNT**_

### 

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/performance-tuning#intermedium_mint_from_file)

INTERMEDIUM\_MINT\_FROM\_FILE

For an arb trade(A ->B ->A), B is called intermedium mint here. Instead of using tokens pulled from Birdeye, you can also add your own mints that you want to use as the intermedium mints. This can be helpful when you noticed a token that is has potential but don't have enough volume yet, or there's a big token launch coming and you just want to prepare for it.

If you don't want to use any mints pulled from Birdeye, you can do that by setting `INTERMEDIUM_MINT_COUNT_FROM_BIRDEYE`to 0, and add all the mints you want to use to`` intermedium-mints.json and set it in `INTERMEDIUM_MINT_FROM_FILE` ``

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/performance-tuning#bot)

Bot


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The last step is tuning your bot. There's a lot of trade offs to make here, so you will likely need to test different combinations your self and find the best strategy that fits you.

### 

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/performance-tuning#quote-time)

Quote time

You should see the quote time for all your opportunities in the log. This will give you some idea on how fast you are talking to your jupiter server.

In general, if you only do 2hop, USE\_DIRECT\_ROUTE\_ONLY, a good quote time is under 10ms, 30ms is acceptable.

If you do 3hop, or USE\_DIRECT\_ROUTE\_ONLY = false, a good quote time is under 200ms, 300ms is acceptable but not idea.

If you are seeing consistent high number, you should tune it. See [My jupiter quote time is high](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/trouble-shooting#my-jupiter-quote-time-is-high)

### 

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/performance-tuning#enable_simulation)

**ENABLE\_SIMULATION**

When this is set to true, all the potential arbs will call a simulationTransaction call to your read RPC, and only the ones that succeeded will be seen as an oppotunity. Running simulation can be very expensive for RPC, so if you have too many pairs of base-mint + trade size, and have a very small PROCESS\_DELAY, this can kill your RPC and causing you to see no opportunities at all.

The good part of setting this to true is, this can greatly reduce the number of failed transactions you land compare to set it to false, but in exchange for an additional call to your RPC which can slow down your speed to send transaction.

When setting this to false, and if you have ENABLE\_SPAM=true, do expect to see a lot of failed transactions.

### 

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/performance-tuning#auto_restart)

**AUTO\_RESTART**

Bot can be set to automatically restart on a fixed time, this can be very helpful to catch the latest trend, when using with birdeye together. Though the restart itself may take a little time, so you will lose the oppotunities during the restart.

### 

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/performance-tuning#process_delay)

**PROCESS\_DELAY**

Process delay means, for each mint + trade size, when the bot finished looking for arb for it, how long does the bot wait until it tries again. Setting a small number here, when you also have a large number of trade size + intermedium mints, can lead to a huge load to your RPC. If you tune this to a small number and stops seeing opportunities, this is what happening.

### 

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/performance-tuning#base_mints)

**BASE\_MINTS**

SolanaMevBot provides several different ways to set trade sizes. You can use fixed trade sizes or using random ones within a range. When you set your trade size, you should try to make it spread over a large range, so it can get all possible opportunities.

e.g. If you have 100 SOL in your wallet, a good distribution can be like this:

1 SOL/2.5 SOL/5 SOL/10 SOL/25 SOL/50 SOL/100 SOL

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/performance-tuning#multiple-locations)

Multiple locations


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you already have a profitable setup, the easiest way to levelup is to duplicate it in different locations! Solana is a decentralized blockchain, a server in Asia may as a ping of >200ms to a server in U.S. By having more machines in different locations you are likely to get much more opportunities in time.

**Note**: If you want to use the same wallet for multiple locations, you should set [`USE_SEPARATE_TIP_ACCOUNT`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#use_separate_tip_account)
 to true. Jito is rate limiting based on ip + wallet/region, this flag can get around this and let you be limited only by ip. You can also use different wallets for different locations.

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/performance-tuning#strategy)

Strategy


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are a lot of strategies you can use with the bot. Some of the examples are listed in [Strategy](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/performance-tuning#strategy)
. And that is just a list of examples.

Different strategies can lead to a huge difference in your profitability. If there's a super volatile token on the market with huge volume, the [Super spam strategy with only 1 or 2 mints](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-strategy#super-spam-strategy-with-only-1-or-2-mints)
can work greatly and generates a lot of profits in a short time period. But the same strategy may not work or even lose you money when the market is dry. You need to test with your specific setup and figure out what's the best strategy for you, and switch it based on market conditions.

[PreviousCommon workflow](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/common-workflow)
[NextBot Strategy](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-strategy)

# Config examples | SolanaMevBot

**If you are a new user, use the** `**Demo account config**` **here. DO NOT USE ANY OTHER ONES.**

Demo account config The [demo account](https://solscan.io/account/DemopzRfMHVjhR9RCPnhg45CtSt85uvSbxgTgN9Sq4Px)
 is using a Jito only strategy. With this strategy you won't land any failed transaction, and can work well with just one RPC. It purely uses RPC and gRPC(Yellowstone) from [Shyft.to](https://shyft.to/)
[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations/config-examples#demo-account-config-the-demo-account-is-using-a-jito-only-strategy.-with-this-strategy-you-wont-land)

The demo account is using a teraswitch machine(8 Core/32GB) in Amsterdam($150/m).

To run this config you need at least ~0.2 sol in your wallet.

Fill in the following field in the config.yaml file(YELLOWSTONE is optional but recommended)

Copy

    KEYS:
      PRIVATE_KEY:
    YELLOWSTONE:
      YELLOWSTONE_URL:
      YELLOWSTONE_XTOKEN: 
    BOT:
      RPC_URL: 

**Full config.yaml**

Copy

    KEYS:
      PRIVATE_KEY:
    YELLOWSTONE:
      YELLOWSTONE_URL:
      YELLOWSTONE_XTOKEN: 
    JUPITER:
      JUPITER_URL: http://127.0.0.1:18080
      JUP_MAX_ACCOUNTS: 20
      LOCAL_JUPITER_PORT: 18080
      USE_DIRECT_ROUTE_ONLY: true
      EXCLUDED_DEXES:
        - 6EF8rrecthR5Dkzon8Nwu78hRvfCKubJ14M5uBEwF6P
        - MoonCVVNZFSYkqNXP6bxHLPL6QQJiMagDL3qcqUQTrG
    INTERMEDIUM_MINTS:
      INTERMEDIUM_MINT_LIST:
        - EPjFWdd5AufqSSqeM2qN1xzybapC8G4wEGGkZwyTDt1v
    BOT:
      RPC_URL: 
      AUTO_RESTART: 30
      MAX_COMPUTE_TIME: 500
      ENABLE_SIMULATION: false
      PAY_FEE_WITH_PROFIT: true
    JITO:
      ENABLE_JITO: true
      TIP_STRATEGIES:
        - dynamic
        - fixed
      FIXED_TIP: 50_000
      MAX_TIP: 1_000_000_000
      DYNAMIC_TIP_BP: 9000
      USE_DIFFERENT_TX_FOR_BLOCK_ENGINES: true
      BLOCK_ENGINES:
        - ny
        - amsterdam
        - frankfurt
        - tokyo
        - slc
    BLIND_QUOTE_STRATEGY:
      ENABLE_BLIND_QUOTE_STRATEGY: true
      BASE_MINTS:
        - MINT: So11111111111111111111111111111111111111112
          SKIP_PROFIT_CHECK_FOR_QUOTE: true
          TRADE_SIZES:
            - 100_000_000
          PROCESS_DELAY: 1000

Copy trade config The [Spam account](https://birdeye.so/profile/SpamwqHeYHX5D17wsUBXDLMDDaMpXFSz9HPsZKZi34X?chain=solana)
 is using this config. This is a Jito config that copy the top players' mints and trying to find arb on them. This is just an example and is not a fully tuned config. You may need to adjust based on your setups.[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations/config-examples#copy-trade-config-the-spam-account-is-using-this-config.-this-is-a-jito-config-that-copy-the-top-pla)

[https://www.circular.bot/trends](https://www.circular.bot/trends)
 is a good place to find the current best player.

        - 6EF8rrecthR5Dkzon8Nwu78hRvfCKubJ14M5uBEwF6P

            SUCCESSFUL_ONLY: true # Only consider successful transactions

            TX_COUNT_PER_ADDRESS: 20 # Number of latest transactions to check on start
            SUCCESSFUL_ONLY: true # Only consider successful transactions

            TX_COUNT_PER_ADDRESS: 20 # Number of latest transactions to check on start
            SUCCESSFUL_ONLY: true # Only consider successful transactions
    BOT:
      RPC_URL: ''
      AUTO_RESTART: 30
      MIN_SOL_BALANCE: 10_000_000_000
      MAX_COMPUTE_TIME: 500
      ENABLE_SIMULATION: false

      STATIC_TIP_BP: 8655

      ENABLE_BLIND_QUOTE_STRATEGY: true
      BASE_MINTS:
        - MINT: So11111111111111111111111111111111111111112
          MIN_QUOTE_PROFIT: 500_000
          TRADE_RANGE:
            FROM: 2_000_000_000
            TO: 10_000_000_000
          TRADE_RANGE_COUNT: 3
          TRADE_RANGE_STRATEGY: random
          PROCESS_DELAY: 100
        - MINT: So11111111111111111111111111111111111111112
          MIN_QUOTE_PROFIT: 500_000
          TRADE_RANGE:
            FROM: 10_000_000_000
            TO: 50_000_000_000
          TRADE_RANGE_COUNT: 3
          TRADE_RANGE_STRATEGY: random
          PROCESS_DELAY: 100

Spam config This is an example config for how to use spam strategy. Note you need multiple good RPCs for sending, minimize all possible latencies, and tune it yourself to be profitable with spam strategy. Not everyone can be profitable with spam strategy.[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations/config-examples#spam-config-this-is-an-example-config-for-how-to-use-spam-strategy.-note-you-need-multiple-good-rpcs)

Fill in the following field in the config.yaml file(YELLOWSTONE is optional but recommended)

Copy

    KEYS:
      PRIVATE_KEY:
    YELLOWSTONE:
      YELLOWSTONE_URL:
      YELLOWSTONE_XTOKEN: 
    BOT:
      RPC_URL: 
    SPAM:
      SEND_RPC_URLS:   

**config.yaml**

Copy

    KEYS:
      PRIVATE_KEY: ''
    YELLOWSTONE:
      YELLOWSTONE_URL: ''
      YELLOWSTONE_XTOKEN: ''
    JUPITER:
      MARKET_MODE: remote
      DISABLE_LOCAL_JUPITER: false
      JUPITER_URL: http://0.0.0.0:18080
      JUP_MAX_ACCOUNTS: 20
      LOCAL_JUPITER_PORT: 18080
      USE_DIRECT_ROUTE_ONLY: true
      USE_LOCAL_MARKET_CACHE: false
      EXCLUDED_DEXES:
        - 6EF8rrecthR5Dkzon8Nwu78hRvfCKubJ14M5uBEwF6P
        - MoonCVVNZFSYkqNXP6bxHLPL6QQJiMagDL3qcqUQTrG
    INTERMEDIUM_MINTS:
      INTERMEDIUM_MINT_COUNT_FROM_BIRDEYE: 500
    BOT:
      RPC_URL: ''
      AUTO_RESTART: 60
      MAX_COMPUTE_TIME: 400
      ENABLE_SIMULATION: true
    SPAM:
      ENABLE_SPAM: true
      SPAM_RESTRICT_LEVEL: 0
      SKIP_PREFLIGHT: true
      USE_DIFFERENT_TX_FOR_SENDERS: false
      FIXED_COMPUTE_UNIT_LIMIT: 250000
      COMPUTE_UNIT_PRICE: 10001
      PRIORITY_FEE_UPDATE_INTERVAL: 60
      MAX_RETRIES: 0
      SEND_RPC_URLS: []
      
    BLIND_QUOTE_STRATEGY:
      ENABLE_BLIND_QUOTE_STRATEGY: true
      SKIP_SAME_OPPORTUNITY: true
      BASE_MINTS:
        - MINT: So11111111111111111111111111111111111111112
          MIN_QUOTE_PROFIT: 500_000
          TRADE_RANGE:
            FROM: 1_000_000_000
            TO: 10_000_000_000
          TRADE_RANGE_COUNT: 10
          TRADE_RANGE_STRATEGY: linear
          PROCESS_DELAY: 500
        - MINT: EPjFWdd5AufqSSqeM2qN1xzybapC8G4wEGGkZwyTDt1v
          MIN_QUOTE_PROFIT: 500_000
          TRADE_RANGE:
            FROM: 100_000_000
            TO: 500_000_000
          TRADE_RANGE_COUNT: 5
          TRADE_RANGE_STRATEGY: linear
          PROCESS_DELAY: 500

Super spam config It's using helius and read RPC and helius + quickndoe as send rpcs. This is an example config on how to use super spam strategy. Note you need multiple good RPCs for sending, minimize all possible latencies, and always have an eye on the market for the hottest mint. See [Super spam strategy with only 1 or 2 mints](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-strategy#super-spam-strategy-with-only-1-or-2-mints)
 for more details about this config. The intermedium-mints.json will be updated very frequently so the mints here is likely not the one the bot is using right now. \*_The Spam account is not always active, I periodically turn it off when the market condition is not good for the config._[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations/config-examples#super-spam-config-its-using-helius-and-read-rpc-and-helius--quickndoe-as-send-rpcs.-this-is-an-exam)

Fill in the following field in the config.yaml file(YELLOWSTONE is optional but recommended)

Copy

    KEYS:
      PRIVATE_KEY:
    YELLOWSTONE:
      YELLOWSTONE_URL:
      YELLOWSTONE_XTOKEN: 
    BOT:
      RPC_URL: 
    SPAM:
      SEND_RPC_URLS:  

**config.yaml**

You can also use [flashloan](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#flashloan)
 with this strategy if you don't have enough fund.

Copy

    KEYS:
      PRIVATE_KEY: ''
    YELLOWSTONE:
      YELLOWSTONE_URL: ''
      YELLOWSTONE_XTOKEN: ''
    JUPITER:
      MARKET_MODE: remote
      DISABLE_LOCAL_JUPITER: false
      JUPITER_URL: http://0.0.0.0:18080
      JUP_MAX_ACCOUNTS: 20
      LOCAL_JUPITER_PORT: 18080
      USE_DIRECT_ROUTE_ONLY: true
      USE_LOCAL_MARKET_CACHE: false
      EXCLUDED_DEXES:
        - 6EF8rrecthR5Dkzon8Nwu78hRvfCKubJ14M5uBEwF6P
        - MoonCVVNZFSYkqNXP6bxHLPL6QQJiMagDL3qcqUQTrG
    INTERMEDIUM_MINTS:
      INTERMEDIUM_MINT_COUNT_FROM_BIRDEYE: 0
      INTERMEDIUM_MINT_COUNT_FROM_GECKO: 0
      INTERMEDIUM_MINT_FROM_FILE: intermedium-mints.json
    BOT:
      RPC_URL: ''
      AUTO_RESTART: 60
      MAX_COMPUTE_TIME: 400
      ENABLE_SIMULATION: false

      SPAM_RESTRICT_LEVEL: 0
      SKIP_PREFLIGHT: true

      COMPUTE_UNIT_PRICE: 250000
      PRIORITY_FEE_UPDATE_INTERVAL: 60
      MAX_RETRIES: 0
      SEND_RPC_URLS: []
    JITO:
      ENABLE_JITO: false
      
    BLIND_QUOTE_STRATEGY:
      ENABLE_BLIND_QUOTE_STRATEGY: true
      BASE_MINTS:
        - MINT: So11111111111111111111111111111111111111112
          SKIP_PROFIT_CHECK_FOR_QUOTE: true
          TRADE_RANGE:
            FROM: 1_000_000_000
            TO: 40_000_000_000

**intermedium-mints.json**

You want to put the current hottest mint with lots of volume and velocity here. This is just an example.

Copy

    [\
      "CTJf74cTo3cw8acFP1YXF3QpsQUUBGBjh2k2e8xsZ6UL"\
    ]

High fee backrun config This strategy use a very high gas fee and is sending much less tx than a traditional spam strategy. The goal is to pay a high enough gas fee in order to land fast and catch the opportunity right after it appears. This strategy has the highest requirement for your rpc and server, you want to has as little latency as possible as it may cost you a lot for a fail transaction. This exact config captured the [82 SOL arb](https://solscan.io/tx/39u6y9isQvL776ZpFri9DRQxkckTdE36adwYnFT9QSv9PBCc7KWBy3Pf5y2Emy8bYwfKNMi98tg7RMDezGqHLFNL)
[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations/config-examples#high-fee-backrun-config-this-strategy-use-a-very-high-gas-fee-and-is-sending-much-less-tx-than-a-tra)

config.yaml

[NextCommon workflow](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/common-workflow)

        - Raydium

        - MeteoraDLMM
      MIN_PRICE_IMPACT_PCT: 0.1

        - MINT: So11111111111111111111111111111111111111112
          MIN_SIMULATED_PROFIT: 200_000
          SKIP_PROFIT_CHECK_FOR_QUOTE: true
          MIN_TRADE_SIZE: 500_000_000
          MAX_TRADE_SIZE: 150_000_000_000
          TRADE_CONFIGS:
            - MIN_TRADE_BP: 2000
              MAX_TRADE_BP: 2000
          ROUTE_TYPES:

Release 1.0.0


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-1.0.0.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-1.0.0.zip)

1.0.0 introducing a full automation mode by integrating with Circular. Bot can now automatically monitor for hot mints/pools and runs 24/7 without any user intervention! You no longer need to manually handle lookup tables or change mint/pools. All you have to do is set a detailed config for circular and you are good to go!

*   Bot fee is now 10% instead of 15%!
    
*   A full integration with Circular. See [Circular config](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/bot-configurations/circular-config)
     for more details. You can also get started with a simple example config here: [Use Circular integration(Recommended)](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/bot-configurations/config-examples#use-circular-integration-recommended)
    
*   Introducing a new log config. See [Log](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/bot-configurations#log)
    
*   Introducing a new auto rebalance config. See [Auto rebalance](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/bot-configurations#auto-rebalance)
    
*   Update fee account for pump amm mayhem mode
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/releases#release-0.15.1)

    . When enabled, the bot will send each transaction as its own bundle paying its own tip, instead of all in one bundle.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.8.8.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.8.8.zip)

Release 0.8.7


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.8.7.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.8.7.zip)

*   Fixed an issue when lookup table contains jito tip account, the bot may fail to send bundle.
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/releases#release-0.8.6)

Release 0.8.6


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.8.6.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.8.6.zip)

*   Added spam support for `bundle_group`. Now spam also works with `bundle_group`. Each transaction will still be send out on itself with the fee you set. But you can use merge mint to generate multiple transactions and send out through rpc.
    
*   Added a new optional config `enabled_bundle_groups` for both [jito](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/bot-configurations#enabled_bundle_groups-1)
     and [spam](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/bot-configurations#enabled_bundle_groups)
    . You can now control which group is being sent out by which method more easily.
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/releases#release-0.8.5)

Release 0.8.5


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.8.5.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.8.5.zip)

*   Added [`bundle_group`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/bot-configurations#bundle_group)
     config to `routing.mint_config_list`. You can now bundle up to 5(or 4 if you set `use_separate_tip_account` to true) transactions into one jito bundle and only pay tip once.
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/releases#release-0.8.4)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.8.4.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.8.4.zip)

*   Bump no\_failure\_mode tip limit from 1\_000\_000 to 5\_000\_000

Release 0.8.1


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.8.1.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.8.1.zip)

Release 0.8.0


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.8.0.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.8.0.zip)

*   Removed kamino\_flashloan
    
*   Added buildin `flashloan`. Currently 30 SOL and 5000 USDC is in the flashloan pool. Will slowly increase as more testing conducted.
    
*   Added solfi integration(experimental). Solfi is not open sourced, so the quote function the program uses may not have the exact correct calculation. You can add with `solfi_pool_list` .
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/releases#release-0.7.12)

Release 0.7.10


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.7.10.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.7.10.zip)

*   Added a new tip\_config/compute\_unit\_price strategy `ExponentialRandom`. Similar to Exponential, this is using similar distribution but generate numbers randomly. This can give a better distribution for a large range.
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/releases#release-0.7.9)

Release 0.7.8


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.7.8.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.7.8.zip)

    . It was `OneByOne` before, now you can config it to be `AllAtOnce`.
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/releases#release-0.7.7)

Release 0.7.7


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.7.7.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.7.7.zip)

*   Added a tip cap of 0.001 SOL when enabling `no_failure_mode`.
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/releases#release-0.7.6)

Release 0.7.6


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.7.6.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.7.6.zip)

*   Added a new \[jito\] config [no\_failure\_mode](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/bot-configurations#jito)
    . When this is enabled, tx with no profit will not fail. This is also very uuid friendly as you will have a 100% success rate with it.
    
*   `use_separate_tip_account` will always be set to true when you add ip\_addresses.
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/releases#release-0.7.5)

Release 0.7.1


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.7.1.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.7.1.zip)

Release 0.7.0


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.7.0.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.7.0.zip)

*   Added new [base\_mint](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/bot-configurations#bot)
     config. You can now arb between USDC/X pools.
    
*   Added support for DLMM/Orca Whirlpool, Orca Whirlpool/Orca Whirlpool arb.
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/releases#release-0.6.6)

Release 0.6.6


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.6.6.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.6.6.zip)

*   Added a new [min\_profit](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/bot-configurations#min_profit)
     config for \[jito\]. You can now use this to prevent landing jito transaction that doesn't cover the gas fee.
    
*   Added a new [use\_separate\_tip\_account](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/bot-configurations#use_separate_tip_account)
     config for \[jito\]. This was automatically set to true when you set ip\_addresses previously, but now you need to set it explicitly.
    
*   Added a new File strategy for [\[compute\_unit\_price\]](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/bot-configurations#compute_unit_price)
     and [\[tip\_config\]](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/bot-configurations#tip_config)
    . You can now more easily do automation with dynamic compute unit prices/tips.
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/releases#release-0.6.5)

Release 0.6.5


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.6.5.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.6.5.zip)

*   Fail the command if lookup table creation didn't land.
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/releases#release-0.6.4)

Release 0.6.4


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.6.4.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.6.4.zip)

*   Do not try to extend when the lookup table don't have enough space left.
    
*   Use base64 encoding for rpc sending.
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/releases#release-0.6.3)

Release 0.6.2


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.6.2.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.6.2.zip)

Release 0.6.1


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.6.1.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.6.1.zip)

*   Added [`use_min_profit`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/bot-configurations#use_min_profit)
     flag under jito. By turning this off the onchain program will NOT take your tip amount as min profit, and will land anything that has profit(ignoring tip).
    
*   Added more checks for config files.
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/releases#release-0.6.0)

Release 0.6.0


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.6.0.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.6.0.zip)

*   Add support for Meteora Pool. You can add it with `meteora_damm_pool_list` config. Note: Meteora Pool uses a lot of address, so you always need lookup table when using it.
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/releases#release-0.5.1)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Release 0.5.0


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.5.0.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.5.0.zip)

*   Added support for Raydium CLMM(Centralized Liquidity). You can add it with `raydium_clmm_pool_list` config. Note: Arb between Meteora DLMM/Orca whirlpool/Raydium CLMM is not supported yet.
    
*   Fix a bug with orca pool refresh.
    
*   Added a new `wrap-sol` command to the bot cli. Run `./smb-onchain -h` to see more details.

     config is now similar to jito tip. You can define it with different strategy.

Release 0.3.1


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.3.1.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.3.1.zip)

*   Fix a bug with lookup table creation.
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/releases#release-0.3.0)

Release 0.3.0


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.3.0.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.3.0.zip)

*   **\[Breaking\]**: To run the bot now you need to call `./smb-onchain run config.toml`
    
*   Added a `-h` option to see all the command smb-onchain supports.
    
*   Added several address lookup table related command to smb-onchain. See [Address lookup table](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/address-lookup-table)
     for more details. You can now create and manage your own address lookup table with the smb-onchain cli!
    
*   Added a new \[bot\] config [`merge_mint`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/bot-configurations#merge-mint)
    . This allows you to send one tx to arb multiple mints/pools. This feature is still experimental so please report any issue you saw when using it.
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/releases#release-0.2.5)

Release 0.2.5


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.2.5.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.2.5.zip)

*   Added more config verification logic.
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/releases#release-0.2.4)

Release 0.2.4


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.2.4.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.2.4.zip)

*   Added a lot of config verification logic to make trouble shooting easier.
    
*   Support byte format wallet private key. e.g `[123, 123, ...]`
    
*   **\[BREAKING\]**: `send_rpc_url` is renamed to `send_rpc_urls` and now support multiple sending rpcs.
    
*   Added `max_retries` config for \[spam\]
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/releases#release-0.2.3)

Release 0.2.3


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.2.3.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.2.3.zip)

*   Added Raydium CPMM support. You can now add Pumpfun swap/Raydium AMM/Raydium CPMM/Meteora DLMM together for the same mint. Just add `raydium_cp_pool_list` to your config.
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/releases#release-0.2.2)

Release 0.2.2


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.2.2.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.2.2.zip)

*   Slightly improved how CU is used when using kamino.
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/releases#release-0.2.1)

Release 0.2.1


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.2.1.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.2.1.zip)

*   Added back raydium support. You can now add pump swap/raydium amm/meteora dlmm together for the same mint.
    
*   Added [`compute_unit_limit`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/bot-configurations#bot)
     config under \[bot\]. This is now a required param.
    
*   A lot of bug fixes on how the optimal trade size is calculated. The calculation now is much more accurate.
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/releases#release-0.2.0)

Release 0.2.0


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.2.0.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.2.0.zip)

*   Added pump fun swap support.
    

**NOTE**: This version does not support raydium anymore. It will be added back later. If you want to use the bot for raydium/dlmm please use 0.1.3 instead.

**NOTE**: As this is the first release for pump fun swap support, it's expected to have a lot of bugs. If you are not comfortable testing a beta release please wait until it gets more stable.

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/releases#release-0.1.3)

Release 0.1.3


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.1.3.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.1.3.zip)

*   Fixed a bug with CIDR format ips
    
*   Removed skip\_prefight config
    
*   Added `enable_simple_send` config. You should only set this to true if the default sending doesn't work for you.
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/releases#release-0.1.2)

Release 0.1.2


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.1.2.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.1.2.zip)

*   Allow http connection for jito url.
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/releases#release-0.1.1)

Release 0.1.1


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.1.1.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.1.1.zip)

*   Fix a bug where tx send through jito may not cover the cost of basic gas.
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/releases#release-0.1.0)

Release 0.1.0


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.1.0.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.1.0.zip)

*   **\[Breaking change\]**: tip\_amount is removed. Now a new [tip config](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/bot-configurations#tip-config)
     is used instead.
    
*   Added more logs.
    
*   ips for jito now will be used in random orders.
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/releases#release-0.0.12)

Release 0.0.12


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.0.11.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.0.11.zip)

*   Fixed a bug for sending with jito.
    
*   Added more log for jito.
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/releases#release-0.0.11)

Release 0.0.11


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.0.11.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.0.11.zip)

Release 0.0.10


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.0.10.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.0.10.zip)

*   Add jito uuid support
    
*   Add jito multiple ips support
    
*   Add better error handling
    
*   Add config for `skip_preflight`
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/releases#release-0.0.9)

Release 0.0.9


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.0.9.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.0.9.zip)

*   Added [kamino flashloan support](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/bot-configurations#kamino-flashloan)
    .
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/releases#release-0.0.8)

Release 0.0.8


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.0.8.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.0.8.zip)

*   Support multiple meteora dlmm pool in one mint. You will need to set an address lookup table if you use more than two dlmm pool. see [Bot configurations](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/bot-configurations)
     for more details
    
*   Jito now works with single ip. It still doesn't work with ip rotation setup locally yet.
    
*   Fix a bug with dlmm refresh.
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/releases#release-0.0.7)

Release 0.0.7


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.0.7.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbotonchain/files/smb-onchain-0.0.7.zip)

*   Added key encryption
    
*   Fix a bug with dlmm bin refresh
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/onchain-bot/releases#release-0.0.5)

     to see how to use it.

     param. You can use this to manually select which ips to use for jito.
    
*   Added [`TEMPORAL_REGION_LIST`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#temporal_region_list)
    , [`NEXTBLOCK_REGION_LIST`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#nextblock_region_list)
    , [`BLOXROUTE_REGION_LIST`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#bloxroute_region_list)
    . You can use them to send to multiple regions for a provider.

Release 1.3.12


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-1.3.12.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-1.3.12.zip)

*   Added support for third party Jupiter API
    
    *   Added new config [`JUPITER_API_KEY`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#jupiter_api_key)
        . If your provider uses `x-api-key` in the header, you can set it with this. E.g. Shyft
        
    *   Added new config [`SKIP_JUPITER_TOKEN_LIST_CHECK`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#skip_jupiter_token_list_check)
        . Some provider does not expose their /tokens Jupiter api call, in such case you can set this to true to get around it. E.g. Shyft
        
    *   Added new config [`ADDITIONAL_JUPITER_URL_PARAMS`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#additional_jupiter_url_params)
        . If your provider uses url params for api key, you can set it with this. E.g. `apikey=123456`
        
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/releases#release-1.3.11)

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-1.3.1.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-1.3.1.zip)

Release 1.3.0


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-1.3.0.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-1.3.0.zip)

*   Updated to use a new onchain program. Now an account will be created the first time you run the bot, which will cost ~0.001 SOL. The bot will no longer creating a temp account in every tx. This also brings some nice optimization and reduced the overall size of the transaction.
    
*   New flashloan provider: [`kamino`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#kamino)
    . There is no fee for kamino flashloan, so you can go as high as the kamino vault allows. All three base mints SOL/USDC/USDT are supported. This does increase the CU by about 80,000, and may generate too large of a tx if you are using direct only false. Example tx: [https://solscan.io/tx/3o83KouSGE2tYzm7FgrPyXDpQozcytwEDZ8g1UBBn6aUrJoRXQmQUz2d56iHymmobCGy54YhKF9DKzxPnAHxLxEj](https://solscan.io/tx/3o83KouSGE2tYzm7FgrPyXDpQozcytwEDZ8g1UBBn6aUrJoRXQmQUz2d56iHymmobCGy54YhKF9DKzxPnAHxLxEj)
    
*   Update the script to support http://127.0.0.1 as the local jupiter url.
    
*   Support `SolFi` for backrun [DEXES\_TO\_MONITOR](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#dexes_to_monitor)
    
*   Added new config [INTERMEDIUM\_MINT\_FROM\_FILES](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#intermedium_mint_from_files)
    , which takes a list of files and merge the mints in them
    
*   Added new config [INTERMEDIUM\_MINT\_LIST](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#intermedium_mint_list)
    , which is just a list of mints. You no longer need to create a file if you just want to run a few mints manually selected.
    
*   Bug fixes
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/releases#release-1.2.3)

Release 1.1.2


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-1.1.2.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-1.1.2.zip)

*   `./run.sh` now can take a param as the config you use. This can make it easier to switch between different configs. example: `./run.sh config.jito.yaml`
    
*   Added a new config [`INTERMEDIUM_MINT_COUNT_FROM_JUPITER`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#intermedium_mint_count_from_jupiter)
    . This is only useful when you connect to a remote Jupiter. Example usage is running multiple bot with the same Jupiter server.
    
*   Added a new option to only send through jito for several sending venders:
    
    *   [NEXTBLOCK\_JITO\_ONLY](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#nextblock_jito_only)
        
    *   [FAST\_JITO\_ONLY](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#fast_jito_only)
        
    *   [BLOXROUTE\_JITO\_ONLY](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#bloxroute_jito_only)
        
    
*   Add support for sending through Jito GRPC. You should only look into this if you have a Jito GRPC key. See [`ENABLE_JITO_GRPC`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#enable_jito_grpc)
     for more detail.
    
*   Bug fixes
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/releases#release-1.1.0)

*   Update how static/fixed tip strategy work when `USE_SEPARATE_TIP_ACCOUNT` is enabled to better prepare for jito's update. It's now static tipping when you use static/fixed tip strategy with `USE_SEPARATE_TIP_ACCOUNT`
    
*   Upgrade the default jupiter version to [v6.0.35](https://github.com/jup-ag/jupiter-swap-api/releases/tag/v6.0.35)

Release 1.0.25


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-1.0.25.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-1.0.25.zip)

*   Fixed a bug with `MIN_COMPUTE_UNIT_PRICE`
    
*   Fixed a bug with max trade size when using `TRADE_SIZES`
    
*   Added a new param [`COMPUTE_UNIT_LIMIT_MULTIPLIER`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#compute_unit_limit_multiplier)
    .
    
*   Update how the default compute unit limit is calculated.
    
*   Added a new `TRADE_RANGE_STRATEGY`: `exponential`. For example for range 10-1000, with a count 5, it will generate the following trade sizes: \[10, 77, 315, 668, 1000\]

Release 1.0.24


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-1.0.24.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-1.0.24.zip)

*   Added config to hide vender failure logs. `TEMPORAL_SHOW_SENDING_ERROR`, `NEXTBLOCK_SHOW_SENDING_ERROR`, `FAST_SHOW_SENDING_ERROR`
    
*   Added config to set max fee for venders. `BLOXROUTE_MAX_DYNAMIC_FEE`, `TEMPORAL_MAX_DYNAMIC_FEE`, `FAST_MAX_DYNAMIC_FEE`, `NEXTBLOCK_MAX_DYNAMIC_FEE`
    
*   Bug fixes
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/releases#release-1.0.23)

Release 1.0.20


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-1.0.20.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-1.0.20.zip)

*   Optimize jupiter quote time, you should see at least 10% improvement on the quote time.
    
*   Added a new config [`JUPITER_WORKER_COUNT`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#jupiter_worker_count)
     to config how many workers(thread) to use for fetching from Jupiter.
    
*   Optimize 3hop quote logic, you should see a much better quote time now compare to previously.
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/releases#release-1.0.19)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-1.0.19.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-1.0.19.zip)

*   Fixed a bug with max tip not applied for static tip
    
*   Optimized compute unit
    
*   Added a new config [MIN\_COMPUTE\_UNIT\_PRICE](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#min_compute_unit_price)
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/releases#release-1.0.18)

Release 1.0.18


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-1.0.18.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-1.0.18.zip)

*   Added a new feature [INTERMEDIUM\_MINT\_FILTER](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#intermedium_mint_filter)
    . This is useful when you run multiple machines and want to use different mints for them.
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/releases#release-1.0.17)

Release 1.0.17


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-1.0.17.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-1.0.17.zip)

*   Added a new experimental feature [BIND\_IP](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#bind_ip)
    . If your server has multiple public ips you can set it with the config to have more jito rate limit, do remember to use this together with [USE\_SEPARATE\_TIP\_ACCOUNT](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#use_separate_tip_account)
    
*   You can now set the fee paid to sending venders BloXRoute/NextBlock/Temporal based on your projected profit. Check the according config docs
    
    *   [BLOXROUTE\_DYNAMIC\_FEE](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#bloxroute_dynamic_fee)
        , [BLOXROUTE\_DYNAMIC\_FEE\_BP](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#bloxroute_dynamic_fee_bp)
        
    *   [NEXTBLOCK\_DYNAMIC\_FEE](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#nextblock_dynamic_fee)
        , [NEXTBLOCK\_DYNAMIC\_FEE\_BP](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#nextblock_dynamic_fee_bp)
        
    *   [TEMPORAL\_DYNAMIC\_FEE](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#temporal_dynamic_fee)
        , [TEMPORAL\_DYNAMIC\_FEE\_BP](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#temporal_dynamic_fee_bp)
        
    
*   Added a new script [upgrade-jup.sh](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/common-workflow#upgrade-downgrade-jupiter-api-version)
     so you can upgrade/downgrade jupiter versions as you wish.
    
*   If you have API key from circular.bot, you can now directly use their api with the bot. See [INTERMEDIUM\_MINT\_FROM\_CIRCULAR](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#intermedium_mint_from_circular)
    
*   Bug fixes
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/releases#release-1.0.16)

Release 1.0.9


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-1.0.9.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-1.0.9.zip)

*   The bot will now remove intermedium mints that keep failing to quote for 50 times in a row.
    
*   A new config [`ROUTE_TYPES`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#route_types)
     for `BLIND_QUOTE_STRATEGY` is added. This allows similar routes like setting [`USE_DIRECT_ROUTE_ONLY`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#use_direct_route_only)
     to false, but with a much faster quote time. Read the doc for more details and example.
    
*   Fix a bug with helius where it shouldn't fetch when it's not enabled
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/releases#release-1.0.8)

Release 1.0.8


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-1.0.8.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-1.0.8.zip)

*   Starting from 1.0.8 the bot will encrypt your private key into a file called `ENCRYPT_PRIVATE_KEY` on your first run, and ask you to remove your private key config once it's created. Though this is not 100% bullet proof but it does make it harder for hackers to get access to your key on the vps. You can disable this behavior by setting the [`ENCRYPT_PRIVATE_KEY`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#encrypt_private_key)
     to false.
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/releases#release-1.0.7)

Release 1.0.7


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-1.0.7.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-1.0.7.zip)

*   Support custom BloXRoute key. You can now set [`BLOXROUTE_KEY`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#bloxroute_key)
     to use your own key with no rate limit.
    
*   Support a new 3rd party send transaction provider [`NEXTBLOCK`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#nextblock)
    . Check config doc for more details. [https://nextblock.io/](https://nextblock.io/)
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/releases#release-1.0.6)

*   BloXRoute rate limit is now set to 10/s, as we have more and more people using it.

Release 1.0.0


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-1.0.0.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-1.0.0.zip)

This is a big release with multiple breaking changes. Please read the release note here carefully before upgrading. You can use the example config inside [bot configuration](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations)
 page or the `config.yaml.example` file come with the bot as a reference.

1.0.0 introduced a new strategy [`BACKRUN_STRATEGY`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#backrun_strategy)
, which introduces a whole new way to find opportunities. The [82 SOL arb](https://solscan.io/tx/39u6y9isQvL776ZpFri9DRQxkckTdE36adwYnFT9QSv9PBCc7KWBy3Pf5y2Emy8bYwfKNMi98tg7RMDezGqHLFNL)
 is landed with this new strategy. Read the docs on the strategy to learn more.

The old way of running the bot is now renamed into [`BLIND_QUOTE_STRATEGY`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#blind_quote_strategy)
.

Changes to old config

*   [`BASE_MINTS`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#base_mints)
     is now moved under [`BLIND_QUOTE_STRATEGY`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#blind_quote_strategy)
    
*   [`SPAM_FEE_BPS`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#spam_fee_bps)
     and [`PRIORITY_FEE_PERCENTILE`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#priority_fee_percentile)
     is now moved to [`SPAM`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#spam)
    
*   `BIRDEYE_API_KEY` is deprecated. You no longer need it to get birdeye tokens.
    
*   [`PROCESS_DELAY`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#process_delay)
     is moved to [`BASE_MINTS`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#base_mints)
     under [`BLIND_QUOTE_STRATEGY`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#blind_quote_strategy)
    
*   `MAX_PRIORITY_FEE` is moved to `SPAM` and renamed to `MAX_COMPUTE_UNIT_PRICE`
    
*   `MIN_PROFIT` is renamed to [`MIN_QUOTE_PROFIT`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#min_quote_profit)
    
*   `SKIP_SAME_OPPORTUNITY` is now moved under [`BLIND_QUOTE_STRATEGY`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#blind_quote_strategy)
    
*   `TRADE_SIZE` is rename to `TRADE_SIZES`
    

Other changes with the release

*   Update jupiter api to [v6.0.33](https://github.com/jup-ag/jupiter-swap-api/releases/tag/v6.0.33)
    
*   Improved how jupiter quote works to slightly speed up the quote latency
    
*   Added a new field [`PRIORITY_FEE_STRATEGY`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#priority_fee_strategy)
    . You now need to specifically set which strategy you use similar to jito tip.
    
*   Added a new [`BLOXROUTE_FEE`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#bloxroute_fee)
     field inside [`BLOXROUTE`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#bloxroute)
    . You can now increase the BloXRoute fee you pay
    
*   Added a new [`ENABLE_SENDING_LOG`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#enable_sending_log)
     field inside [`LOGGING`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#logging)
    . You can now turn off the sending logs in your output.
    
*   Added a new [`MEMO`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#memo-1)
     field inside [`BLIND_QUOTE_STRATEGY`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#blind_quote_strategy)
    . This will override the `MEMO` under `BOT`.
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/releases#release-0.3.14)

Release 0.3.14


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-0.3.14.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-0.3.14.zip)

*   Added [`DOWNLOAD_RPC_URL`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#download_rpc_url)
     and [`DOWNLOAD_RPC_RATE_LIMIT_PER_SECOND`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#download_rpc_rate_limit_per_second)
     param to get around the rpcs that does not support transaction history. You can use a free helius plan now for this.
    
*   Cleanup some logs.
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/releases#release-0.3.13)

Release 0.3.12


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-0.3.12.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-0.3.12.zip)

*   Added a new way to fetch intermedium tokens [`INTERMEDIUM_MINT_COUNT_FROM_BIRDEYE_TRENDING`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#intermedium_mint_count_from_birdeye_trending)
    . You do not need birdeye api to fetch this, this is fetched from bot's own backend. This list has new mints faster than the original birdeye 24h volume list.

Release 0.3.10


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-0.3.10.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-0.3.10.zip)

*   Added a new [`TIP_STRATEGIES`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#tip_strategies)
     field to JITO config. Together with [`STATIC_TIP_BP`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#static_tip_bp)
     as a new param. Read the configuration doc for more details.
    
*   **Breaking**: `JITO_TIP_BP` is now renamed to [`DYNAMIC_TIP_BP`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#dynamic_tip_bp)
    . `JITO_TIP_BP` will still work for now, but changing the name is recommended.
    
*   Fix some config override bug with JITO\_UUID and BLOCK\_ENGINE.
    
*   Cleanup some logs
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/releases#release-0.3.9)

Release 0.3.9


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-0.3.9.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-0.3.9.zip)

*   Update jupiter api to [v6.0.30](https://github.com/jup-ag/jupiter-swap-api/releases/tag/v6.0.30)
    . market mode `europa` may finally be possible to run.
    
*   Fixed a bug with `USE_DIFFERENT_TX_FOR_SENDERS` + flashloan.
    
*   MEMO now also works for flashloan enabled tx
    
*   Added a new config [`PAY_FEE_WITH_PROFIT`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#pay_fee_with_profit)
    . When enabled, for SOL base mint, bot will pay the jito tip/bot fee using your profit. This will allow catching bigger opportunitiese even when you don't have enough SOL balance to pay for jito tip.
    

![](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3811539071-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fx2rxpD03KDvMgJqIkdla%252Fuploads%252F2kRcFoBsiJWY8fpEbMwt%252FScreenshot%25202024-10-25%2520at%252012.26.07%25E2%2580%25AFAM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8ba84984-e277-4478-8ae7-edbbfd9d3018&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4bbf070&sv=2)

Release 0.3.4


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-0.3.4.zip](https://sourceforge.net/projects/solanamevbot/files/solana-mev-bot-0.3.4.zip)

*   **Breaking**: Changed format of [`INTERMEDIUM_MINT_FROM_ADDRESSES`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#intermedium_mint_from_addresses)
    , now it takes an additional param `MAX_MINT_COUNT`, See [Bot configurations](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#intermedium_mint_from_addresses)
     for more details. This will allow more targeted strategy like only try to arb the mints with the most arbs possible.
    

*   `USE_DIFFERENT_TX_FOR_BLOCK_ENGINES` is now deprecated. Bot will always send different tx to different block engines.
    
*   Added a new JITO config [`MAX_TIP`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#max_tip)
    
*   Added a new JITO config [`FIXED_TIP`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#fixed_tip)
     . Note this is NOT sharing the jito rate limit as using `JITO_TIP_BP`, and can be config together with `JITO_TIP_BP` or alone by itself.
    
*   Fix a bug with [`INTERMEDIUM_MINT_FROM_ADDRESSES`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#intermedium_mint_from_addresses)
     that some address failed to load.
    
*   Optimize the logic for [`INTERMEDIUM_MINT_COUNT_FROM_GECKO`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#intermedium_mint_count_from_gecko)
    . Note [`INTERMEDIUM_MINT_COUNT_FROM_GECKO`](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#intermedium_mint_count_from_gecko)
     can only return ~20-30 mints at maximum due to their limitation on the api.
    
*   Show log for `run-jup.sh` script.
    
*   Added a new capability to override JITO/SPAM config within BASE\_MINT, see [config override](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/bot-configurations#config-override)
     for more details. This basically allows you to override the global value for each base mint you define. Here's an example that override the `JITO_TIP_BP` value for this specific base mint config.
    

[](https://docs.solanamevbot.com/home/deprecated/jupiter-bot/releases#release-0.3.3)
